<div class="output_wrapper" id="output_wrapper_id" style="font-size: 16px; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); line-height: 1.6; word-spacing: 0px; letter-spacing: 0px; font-family: 'Helvetica Neue', Helvetica, 'Hiragino Sans GB', 'Microsoft YaHei', Arial, sans-serif;"><h1 id="h" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.6em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">硬禾学堂雪花灯实验报告: 苏州圣诞来点雪~</span></h1>
<h2 id="h-1" style="line-height: inherit; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.4em; margin-bottom: 2em; margin-right: 5px; padding: 8px 15px; letter-spacing: 2px; background-image: linear-gradient(to right bottom, rgb(0, 188, 212), rgb(63, 81, 181)); background-color: rgb(63, 81, 181); color: rgb(255, 255, 255); border-left: 10px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 5px; text-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 1px; box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 2px;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">导言</span></h2>
<h3 id="h-2" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">背景</span></h3>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">嵌入式系统（Embedded System），是一种嵌入机械或电气系统内部、具有专一功能和实时计算性能的计算机系统[1]。在以5G，物联网，边缘计算，为代表的新的计算浪潮下，掌握嵌入式系统的是成为全栈开发的必要条件，西浦国际创新港携手硬禾学堂，结合研发技术的行业需求和发展趋势，共同推出全栈技能人才培养计划。本报告为雪花灯实验报告，旨在学习嵌入式系统编程的基本开发流程，并且对于嵌入式系统模块和功能有进一步的认识[2]。今天正好是2020圣诞节，这个可爱的雪花灯实验报告，就圣诞礼物送给大家啦~</p>
<h3 id="h-3" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">报告结构</span></h3>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">本报告首先介绍嵌入式系统的基本背景，并且把介绍嵌入式系统的系统架构和实践方法，进而，实验过程和对应的实验结果会呗阐明，最终实验总结和未来展望会被阐述作为报告结尾。</p>
<h2 id="h-4" style="line-height: inherit; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.4em; margin-bottom: 2em; margin-right: 5px; padding: 8px 15px; letter-spacing: 2px; background-image: linear-gradient(to right bottom, rgb(0, 188, 212), rgb(63, 81, 181)); background-color: rgb(63, 81, 181); color: rgb(255, 255, 255); border-left: 10px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 5px; text-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 1px; box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 2px;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">名词表（这里是概念）</span></h2>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">MCU</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">是微处理器Microprocessor的缩写</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">ELEC211要好好学哈，我们用的是ARM Cortex M7来讲的</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">常见的微处理器包括树莓派，Arduino</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">雪花灯：ws2812</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">本质上是一种灯的结构</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225124602391.png" alt="雪花灯原理图" title="雪花灯原理图" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">雪花灯原理图</figcaption></figure></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">WS2812, 这LED内部已经整合了信号处理的芯片</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;">他有四个引脚，分别是<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">VDD作为电源来实现供电管脚</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">DOUT，作为data out 的缩写，作为数据输出的管脚来控制数据信号的输出</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">VSS，作为Voltage Source Source的缩写，是Vdd反过来的兄弟，所以这个是地啦</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">DIN，是data in 的缩写，作为数据输入的管脚，来控制数据信号的输入</span></li></ul></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">具体的线路图在左边，供参考</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">单片机：stc15w204s</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225125353808.png" alt="stc15w204s原理引脚图" title="stc15w204s原理引脚图" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">stc15w204s原理引脚图</figcaption></figure></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">51单片机，STC牛的！</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">我的理解这是一个深圳软件厂家STC做的非常硬核的，成本非常低，非常适合教学的芯片，我们就用这个了。</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">nop()和33M时钟</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">一个nop就是一个指令周期， STC15W204S是1T单片机，所以就是一个机械周期就是一个时钟周期所以在33MHz的情况下，一个nop大概是31ns左右</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">这样20个nop就是610ns，PPT写的是680ns，可能是为了数字好听的工程考虑吧~</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225130034342.png" alt="nop分析图表" title="nop分析图表" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">nop分析图表</figcaption></figure></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">这里有一个PPT，我其实并不知道如何调出这个窗口？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">至于所谓的33MHz，我们可以通过这个下拉窗口来实现</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225130144297.png" alt="stc时序设置模块" title="stc时序设置模块" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">stc时序设置模块</figcaption></figure></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">话说这个33MHz好像和nop有点关系，但我不知道是什么。</span></li>
</ul>
<h2 id="h-5" style="line-height: inherit; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.4em; margin-bottom: 2em; margin-right: 5px; padding: 8px 15px; letter-spacing: 2px; background-image: linear-gradient(to right bottom, rgb(0, 188, 212), rgb(63, 81, 181)); background-color: rgb(63, 81, 181); color: rgb(255, 255, 255); border-left: 10px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 5px; text-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 1px; box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 2px;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">方法论</span></h2>
<h3 id="h-6" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">嵌入式系统整体结构</span></h3>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201223194520233.png" alt="通用嵌入式系统与外界环境交互范式" title="通用嵌入式系统与外界环境交互范式" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">通用嵌入式系统与外界环境交互范式</figcaption></figure></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">我们的世界是模拟的世界，也就是连续的世界</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">这样我们从传感器把自然界的信号转换成电信号</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">之后我们通过放大，滤波，我们得到了对于我们有意义的信号</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">之后，我们通过多路转换，采样保持，做一些转换和convert</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">之后我们到了A2D的东西，这样我们生成了数字信号，输入到微信计算机的输入接口里面</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">之后计算机通过它的强大 的计算能力，产生了对应的输出信号</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">通过D2A</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">我们通过放大，驱动，我们到了机械臂，来做相对应的执行</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">改变这个连续的世界！</span></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="h-7" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">嵌入式系统实践：雪花灯控制系统</span></h3>
<figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225124104650.png" alt="雪花灯控制系统" title="雪花灯控制系统" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">雪花灯控制系统</figcaption></figure>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">我们通过PC串口助手上把编好的程序以hex文件的形式</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">通过UART的传输协议</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">传送到MCU，也就是微处理器上面</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">微处理器通过程序来选择WS2812灯亮灭的方式</span></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="h-8" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">数据传输方式</span></h3>
<figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225125218122.png" alt="UART数据传输方式解释" title="UART数据传输方式解释" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">UART数据传输方式解释</figcaption></figure>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">我的理解这个数据他能同时有四个口传，总共有24bit的数据传输结构，长楼上这个样子。</p>
<h3 id="h-9" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">点亮雪花板</span></h3>
<figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225125647469.png" alt="点亮雪花板的状态和码的对应关系" title="点亮雪花板的状态和码的对应关系" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">点亮雪花板的状态和码的对应关系</figcaption></figure>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">说实话，这个板子插上去就亮了，我也不知道这个数据传输时间在这里是怎么体现的。。。</p>
<h3 id="h-10" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">编程啦</span></h3>
<h4 id="h-11" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">串口初始化</span></h4>
<pre style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><code class="c++ language-c++ hljs cpp" style="overflow-wrap: break-word; margin: 0px 2px; line-height: 18px; font-size: 14px; font-weight: normal; word-spacing: 0px; letter-spacing: 0px; font-family: Consolas, Inconsolata, Courier, monospace; border-radius: 0px; color: rgb(169, 183, 198); background: rgb(40, 43, 46); overflow-x: auto; padding: 0.5em; white-space: pre !important; word-wrap: normal !important; word-break: normal !important; overflow: auto !important; display: -webkit-box !important;"><span class="hljs-function" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(248, 35, 117); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;"><span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(248, 35, 117); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">void</span>&nbsp;<span class="hljs-title" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(165, 218, 45); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">UartInit</span><span class="hljs-params" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(255, 152, 35); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">(<span class="hljs-keyword" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(248, 35, 117); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">void</span>)</span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<span class="hljs-comment" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(128, 128, 128); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">//9600bps@33MHz</span><br></span>{<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;SCON&nbsp;=&nbsp;<span class="hljs-number" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(174, 135, 250); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">0x50</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;AUXR&nbsp;|=&nbsp;<span class="hljs-number" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(174, 135, 250); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">0x01</span>;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;<br>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;AUXR&nbsp;|=&nbsp;<span class="hljs-number" style="font-size: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; color: rgb(174, 135, 250); word-wrap: inherit !important; word-break: inherit !important;">1</span>;<br>}<br></code></pre>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">初始化哈</p>
<h4 id="hscon" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><strong style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; font-weight: bold;">SCON</strong>寄存器</span></h4>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">好像要把这个寄存器取个值SCON=0x50;//0101 0000</span></li>
</ul>
<h4 id="h1" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">串口1的四种工作方式的定义方式</span></h4>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">SM0=0 SM1=0</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">SM0=0 SM1=1</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">SM0=1 SM1=0</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">SM0=1 SM1=1</span></li>
</ul>
<h4 id="h-12" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.2em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">最后一个比较重要的代码块</span></h4>
<figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225130810294.png" alt="UART传输协议代码块" title="UART传输协议代码块" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">UART传输协议代码块</figcaption></figure>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">我的理解是这个是一个实现UART接受数据的函数，总之UART用这个就对了。</p>
<h2 id="h-13" style="line-height: inherit; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.4em; margin-bottom: 2em; margin-right: 5px; padding: 8px 15px; letter-spacing: 2px; background-image: linear-gradient(to right bottom, rgb(0, 188, 212), rgb(63, 81, 181)); background-color: rgb(63, 81, 181); color: rgb(255, 255, 255); border-left: 10px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 5px; text-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 1px; box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 2px;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验过程</span></h2>
<h3 id="h-14" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验仪器布局图</span></h3>
<figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225122552532.png" alt="实验仪器布局" title="实验仪器布局" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">实验仪器布局</figcaption></figure>
<h3 id="h1-1" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验过程1</span></h3>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">通过stc的脚本调试工具导入hex文件</p>
<figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225123037679.png" alt="STC调试软件" title="STC调试软件" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">STC调试软件</figcaption></figure>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">在这里要设置灯是ws2812，单片机是stc15w204s，时钟选择33M</p>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">导入的hex文件见附录。</p>
<h3 id="h2" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验过程2</span></h3>

<h2 id="h-15" style="line-height: inherit; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.4em; margin-bottom: 2em; margin-right: 5px; padding: 8px 15px; letter-spacing: 2px; background-image: linear-gradient(to right bottom, rgb(0, 188, 212), rgb(63, 81, 181)); background-color: rgb(63, 81, 181); color: rgb(255, 255, 255); border-left: 10px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 5px; text-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 1px; box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 2px;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验结果</span></h2>
<h3 id="h1-2" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验结果1</span></h3>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">明天十点后</p>
<h3 id="h2-1" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验结果2</span></h3>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">明天十点后</p>
<h3 id="h3-1" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">实验结果3</span></h3>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">明天十点后</p>
<h2 id="h-16" style="line-height: inherit; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.4em; margin-bottom: 2em; margin-right: 5px; padding: 8px 15px; letter-spacing: 2px; background-image: linear-gradient(to right bottom, rgb(0, 188, 212), rgb(63, 81, 181)); background-color: rgb(63, 81, 181); color: rgb(255, 255, 255); border-left: 10px solid rgb(51, 51, 51); border-radius: 5px; text-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 1px; box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 1px 1px 2px;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">总结和未来展望</span></h2>
<h3 id="h-17" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">总结</span></h3>
<p style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px;">人在做事情的时候，要问自己，自己有什么，想要做什么，这个目标的达成需要几个步骤？我能实现其中的几个步骤，这些作为一个迭代，我们再去准备下一个迭代。在这个实验中，我要承认我有几个地方做的不够好，列表如下</p>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">没有上上机实操的课程</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">在12月23日的课程上和同学快速把这个软件进行调试和组装，而把时间放在了概念理解上面(本可以更快的结束这个过程)</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">没有很早的认识到，我们的目标是尽快的把我们能够做到的东西，先做好，之后，再去寻找其他的帮助，来实现下一个level的跨越！强调一下，把自己能够做好的事情做好，作为基础，然后进一步做下一个level的事情。</span></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="h-18" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">未来展望</span></h3>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">调试更多的程序，点亮更多的灯</span></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="h-19" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">疑惑的点</span></h3>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">STC的51的灯和stm32的灯的区别</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">keil4和keil5的区别大么？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">如何使用单片机做到几百ns的延时？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">SCON是干什么的？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">我们要哪一种工作方式？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225130935383.png" alt="SCON寄存器信息" title="SCON寄存器信息" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">SCON寄存器信息</figcaption></figure></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">PCON是做什么的？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">这两个程序分别在哪里写？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225131044354.png" alt="UART初始化和通信信息" title="UART初始化和通信信息" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">UART初始化和通信信息</figcaption></figure></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">所有的UART的协议的波特率都是一样的么？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">这个页面的配置是对的么？</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225133611204.png" alt="Keil4编译配置1" title="Keil4编译配置1" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">Keil4编译配置1</figcaption></figure></li>

<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><figure style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;"><img src="http://qkx5lap40.hn-bkt.clouddn.com/img/image-20201225133703095.png" alt="Keil编译配置2" title="Keil编译配置2" style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; display: block; margin: 0px auto; max-width: 100%;"><figcaption style="line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-top: 10px; text-align: center; color: rgb(153, 153, 153); font-size: 0.7em;">Keil编译配置2</figcaption></figure></li>

</ul>
<h3 id="h-20" style="color: inherit; line-height: inherit; padding: 0px; margin: 1.5em 0px; font-weight: bold; font-size: 1.3em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">要做的事</span></h3>
<ul style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; padding-left: 32px; list-style-type: disc;">
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">把我的报告发给老师</span></li>
<li style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span style="font-size: inherit; color: inherit; line-height: inherit; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">明天上午十点和老师约一下这个自定义程序和接口的实现</span></li>
